width: 0px; height: 4.018em;"></span></span></span></span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-216" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.289em;">=</span><span class="mfrac" id="MathJax-Span-217" style="padding-left: 0.289em;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 0.494em; height: 0px; margin-right: 0.125em; margin-left: 0.125em;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(3.445em, 1000.29em, 4.141em, -999.998em); top: -4.424em; left: 50%; clip: rect(3.404em, 1000.33em, 4.141em, -999.998em); top: -3.645em; left: 50%; margin-left: -0.162em;"><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-219" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">4</span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.018em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(0.904em, 1000.49em, 1.191em, -999.998em); top: -1.268em; left: 0em;"><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: 0em; border-top: 1.5px solid; width: 0.494em; height: 0px;"></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 1.068em;"></span></span></span></span><span class="msubsup" id="MathJax-Span-220"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 1.068em; height: 0px;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(3.199em, 1000.62em, 4.141em, -999.998em); top: -4.014em; left: 0em;"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-221" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">F</span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.018em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; top: -3.85em; left: 0.658em;"><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-222" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">1</span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.018em;"></span></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.018em;"></span></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 6.395em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -5.598em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 6.703em;"></span></span></nobr><span class="MJX_Assistive_MathML" role="presentation"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mi mathvariant="normal">F</mi><mo>∝</mo><mfrac><mn>1</mn><msup><mi mathvariant="normal">d</mi><mn>2</mn></msup></mfrac><mspace linebreak="newline"></mspace><mo stretchy="false">⇒</mo><mfrac><msub><mi mathvariant="normal">F</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><msub><mi mathvariant="normal">F</mi><mn>2</mn></msub></mfrac><mo>=</mo><mfrac><msubsup><mi mathvariant="normal">d</mi><mn>2</mn><mn>2</mn></msubsup><msubsup><mi mathvariant="normal">d</mi><mn>1</mn><mn>2</mn></msubsup></mfrac><mo>=</mo><mfrac><msup><mrow><mo>(</mo><mrow><mn>2</mn><msub><mi mathvariant="normal">d</mi><mn>1</mn></msub></mrow><mo>)</mo></mrow><mn>2</mn></msup><msubsup><mi mathvariant="normal">d</mi><mn>1</mn><mn>2</mn></msubsup></mfrac><mo>=</mo><mn>4</mn><mspace linebreak="newline"></mspace><mo>∴</mo><msub><mi mathvariant="normal">F</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><mo>=</mo><mfrac><mn>1</mn><mn>4</mn></mfrac><msub><mi mathvariant="normal">F</mi><mn>1</mn></msub></math></span></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-12">\rm F\propto\frac{1}{d^2}\\ &nbsp;
\Rightarrow\frac{F_1}{F_2}=\frac{d_2^2}{d_1^2}=\frac{\left(2d_1\right)^2} {d_1^2}=4&nbsp;\\
\therefore F_2=\frac{1}{4}F_1</script></span><br>
[তপন স্যার: সংস্করণ-২০২২, পৃষ্ঠা-৪৫৭]</p>
</span>
                                    </div>

padding-left: 0.289em;">=</span><span class="mfrac" id="MathJax-Span-571" style="padding-left: 0.289em;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 1.846em; height: 0px; margin-right: 0.125em; position: relative; width: 0.822em; height: 0px; margin-right: 0.125em; margin-left: 0.125em;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(3.445em, 1000.29em, 4.141em, -999.998em); top: -4.424em; left: 50%; margin-left: -0.162em;"><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-583" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">1</span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.018em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(3.404em, 1000.7em, 4.141em, -999.998em); top: -3.645em; left: 50%; margin-left: -0.367em;"><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-584" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">64</span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.018em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(0.904em, 1000.82em, 1.191em, -999.998em); top: -1.268em; left: 0em;"><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: 0em; border-top: 1.5px solid; width: 0.822em; height: 0px;"></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 1.068em;"></span></span></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 1.969em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.948em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 2.452em;"></span></span></nobr><span class="MJX_Assistive_MathML" role="presentation"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><msup><mi mathvariant="normal">T</mi><mn>2</mn></msup><mo>∝</mo><msup><mi mathvariant="normal">r</mi><mn>3</mn></msup><mo stretchy="false">⇒</mo><mfrac><msubsup><mi mathvariant="normal">T</mi><mn>1</mn><mn>2</mn></msubsup><msubsup><mi mathvariant="normal">T</mi><mn>2</mn><mn>2</mn></msubsup></mfrac><mo>=</mo><mfrac><msubsup><mi mathvariant="normal">r</mi><mn>1</mn><mn>3</mn></msubsup><msubsup><mi mathvariant="normal">r</mi><mn>2</mn><mn>3</mn></msubsup></mfrac><mo stretchy="false">⇒</mo><mfrac><msubsup><mi mathvariant="normal">T</mi><mn>1</mn><mn>2</mn></msubsup><msubsup><mi mathvariant="normal">T</mi><mn>2</mn><mn>2</mn></msubsup></mfrac><mo>=</mo><mfrac><msup><mi mathvariant="normal">R</mi><mn>3</mn></msup><msup><mrow><mo>(</mo><mrow><mn>4</mn><mi mathvariant="normal">R</mi></mrow><mo>)</mo></mrow><mn>3</mn></msup></mfrac><mo>=</mo><mfrac><msup><mi mathvariant="normal">R</mi><mn>3</mn></msup><mrow><mn>64</mn><mtext>&nbsp;</mtext><msup><mi mathvariant="normal">R</mi><mn>3</mn></msup></mrow></mfrac><mo>=</mo><mfrac><mn>1</mn><mn>64</mn></mfrac></math></span></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-28">\rm T^2\propto r^3\Rightarrow\frac{T_1^2}{T_2^2}=\frac{r_1^3}{r_2^3}\Rightarrow\frac{T_1^2}{T_2^2}=\frac{R^3}{\left(4R\right)^3}=\frac{R^3}{64\ R^3}=\frac{1}{64}&nbsp;</script></span><br>
[ইসহাক স্যার: সংস্করণ-২০২২, পৃষ্ঠা-৪১১]</p>
</span>
                                    </div>
                            </div>

                                        <span style="color: black !important; font-weight: bold;">Solution:</span>
                                        <br>
                                        <span style="color: black !important;"><p>জেনে রাখো: C.G.S পদ্ধতি- মেট্রিক পদ্ধতি, ফ্রেঞ্চ পদ্ধতি, দশমিক পদ্ধতি।<br>
[ইসহাক স্যার: সংস্করণ-২০২২, পৃষ্ঠা-১০]</p>
</span>
                                    </div>
                            </div>
                        </div>

                                    <div class="row solveText" style="display: block; padding:10px; color:#077307; overflow-x: auto; background-color: #d7f7d4;">
                                        <span style="color: black !important; font-weight: bold;">Solution:</span>
                                        <br>
                                        <span style="color: black !important;"><p>জেনে রাখো: বলের দ্বারা কাজ → 0° ≤ θ &lt; 90°<br>
বলের বিরুদ্ধে কাজ → 90°&lt; θ ≤ 180°<br>
শূন্য কাজ →&nbsp;θ = 90°<br>
[ইসহাক স্যার: সংস্করণ-২০২২, পৃষ্ঠা-৩৩৭]</p>
</span>
                                    </div>

                                    <div class="row">
